- `suggested_side` (buy or sell)
- `move_potential_pct` (estimated upside/downside percentage)
- `confidence` (numeric confidence level)
- `veto` (boolean indicating any strong reason to avoid the trade)
- `thesis` (concise rationale focusing on asymmetric upside)

**Constraints**: Emphasize asymmetric upside potential; ensure all relevant data sources are queried before forming the thesis. No execution of trades is requested at this stage.

| **Bid / Ask** | Bid 0.041482 × 1 USDT  ·  Ask 0.041493 × 2 USDT | Very tight spread (≈ 0.000011 USDT) |
| **24‑h High / Low** | High 0.065626 · Low 0.039996 | Price range shows a **‑39 %** swing (high‑low spread ≈ 64 % of low) |
| **24‑h Open** | 0.062772 | Current price is **‑33.9 %** down from open |
| **24‑h Volume** | 234,084 TAC (≈ 23,408,400 USDT) | Strong trading activity, indicating good liquidity |
| **Price Change (24 h)** | **‑33.912 %** | Significant recent sell pressure |

**Key Insights for Trading Decision**

1. **Explosive Move Potential** – The token has dropped ~34 % in one day from its open and is near its 24‑h low, suggesting room for a **reversal rally** if buying pressure returns. A move back toward the 24‑h high (≈ 0.0656) would represent a **~58 % upside** from the current price.

2. **Liquidity** – With > 23 M USDT traded in the last 24 h and a tight bid‑ask spread, the market can accommodate sizable orders without excessive slippage, supporting the doctrine’s need for “real volume”.

3. **Risk Consideration** – The recent sharp decline indicates heightened volatility; a short‑term bounce could be rapid, but the downtrend may continue. Tight risk management (stop ~1 % from entry) is essential.

4. **Funding / Carry** – No funding rate data was retrieved in this call; further checks (e.g., `blofin_get_funding_rate`) are needed to assess any bias from perpetual contracts.

**Potential Trade Thesis**

- **Side:** **Long** (speculating on a corrective rally from the 24‑h low toward the high).
- **Target Move:** 5‑10 %+ intraday gain is realistic; a larger swing toward the 24‑h high could yield > 50 % if momentum returns.
- **Risk:** Tight stop ~1 % below entry; monitor volume and order‑book depth for confirmation.

**Next Steps**

1. Pull **order‑book depth** (`blofin_get_order_book`) to verify depth beyond the top 2 levels.
2. Retrieve **funding rate** (`blofin_get_funding_rate`) for any bias.
3. Run **technical analysis** (`blofin_technical_analysis`) to gauge momentum indicators (RSI, MACD, etc.).
4. If metrics support a strong upside, calculate a **3:1+ reward‑to‑risk** scenario and prepare entry/TP/SL levels.

- **Order‑book snapshot (timestamp ≈ 1.78 × 10¹² ms):**
  - **Best Ask:** 0.3636 USDT for 14,749 WLD
  - **Best Bid:** 0.3635 USDT for 24,578 WLD
- **Depth Imbalance (based on the displayed best‑level volumes):**
  - **Bid side:** 62.5 % of the displayed liquidity
  - **Ask side:** 37.5 % of the displayed liquidity
  - **Net imbalance:** **+0.125** (positive = more buying pressure)

**Key Insights**

1. **Slight buying pressure:** The bid side holds roughly 1.7 × the volume of the ask side, indicating modest bullish sentiment at the top of the book.
2. **Tight spread:** The spread is only 0.0001 USDT (0.027 % of the price), suggesting a highly liquid, actively traded market.
3. **Potential short‑term move:** With a modest bid‑dominant imbalance, a short‑term upward price move is plausible if the pressure sustains.

**Potential Concerns / Errors**

- No errors were reported by the tool; the data appears valid.
- The snapshot reflects only the best level; deeper book data could change the imbalance picture. Use additional depth levels for a more robust assessment.
